5200self as *mut _ as *mut T
5201}
5202#[inline]
5203pub unsafe fn as_slice(&self, len: usize) -> &[T] {
5204::core::slice::from_raw_parts(self.as_ptr(), len)
5205}
5206#[inline]
5207pub unsafe fn as_mut_slice(&mut self, len: usize) -> &mut [T] {

5209}
5210}

5214}
